* Yes, I've taken on new duties
	+ Briefly describe any changes in my role _______________________________________
OR

No significant change; however...

do we need to improve upon for better work-life balance?

Always Most times Some time Rarely Never

**Employee Potentials Questionnaire**

This survey aims at understanding employees' perceived strengths, areas where they need improvement and their overall potential to grow within our organization.

Please answer the questions honestly based upon your current role or responsibilities. Your responses will help us identify opportunities that align with individual goals as well employee development initiatives for future growth

**Section 1: Self-Assessment**

___________________________________________________________________________________________________________

* Communication skills

Time management 

Teamwork collaboration

**Feedback Mechanics Questionnaire**

We're interested in understanding how effective our current feedback mechanisms are and where we can improve them to better support employee growth, development & overall job satisfaction. Your input will help us refine these processes.

Please answer the following questions honestly!

1a) How often do receive constructive criticism or positive reinforcement from your supervisor/manager?

* Daily
	+ Please specify: _______________________
*
Weekly 
+
Monthly  
+

Rarely/Never

[Scale 5-point Likert scale]

2. What types of feedback mechanisms are currently available to you? (Select all that apply)

Regular one-on-one meetings with manager/supervisor 

Anonymous online surveys or forms
Peer-to-peer reviews/evaluations from colleagues/team members 
Written performance evaluations/reviews by supervisor

Other: _______________________________________

3a) How confident do feel in providing constructive feedback yourself?

* Very Confident (Scale 1-5)
	+ Please specify the reasons why you're so sure! _______________________________
*
Somewhat Confidence
+
Neutral/Undecided  
+

Not at all confidence 

[Open-ended text box]

4. What would make it easier for to provide and receive constructive feedback? Select up-to three options:

More frequent check-ins with manager/supervisor 
Clearer expectations on what constitutes "good" or bad performance

Anonymous online surveys/forms
Other: _______________________________________

5a) Have you ever received a piece of negative/constructive criticism that had significant impact (positive/negative)? If yes, please describe the situation:

[Open-ended text box]

6. How important is it for to receive regular feedback on your job satisfaction and performance? Scale 1-10

7b-c: What would be most helpful in improving our current Feedback Mechanisms?

* More frequent check-ins with manager/supervisor 
*
Clearer expectations
+
Anonymous online surveys/forms 

Other suggestions _______________________________________

8. Any additional comments or ideas you'd like to share about the effectiveness of feedback mechanisms within your department/team? ______________________________

Thank You for taking time! Your input is invaluable!

Please let me know if this meets with approval, and I'll be happy assist in converting it into a different format (e.g., Google Forms)
     - User:

**Health &amp; Security Measure Questionnaire**

As part our ongoing efforts in ensuring employee well-being, we would like to gather your thoughts regarding health safety measures within the company. Your input will help us identify areas of improvement.

What do think is most important aspect for maintaining a healthy work environment?

a) Cleanliness
b)
c)

2.)
Have you ever experienced an incident that made me question our health safety measures? If yes, please describe:

3. How often have taken the time to review and familiarize yourself with company's Health &amp; Safety policies?
   Never Rarely Sometimes Often Always

4.
What do think is most effective way for us communicate important updates regarding workplace hazards or incidents?

a) Email
b)
c)

5.)
Have you ever felt pressured by management/colleagues to compromise on health safety measures? If yes, please explain:

6. How confident are in the company's ability respond effectively during an emergency situation?
   Not at all Somewhat Confident Very Comfortable Extremely

7.
What do think is most important factor for ensuring a safe work environment?

a) Proper training
b)
c)

8.)
Have you ever witnessed any near-miss incidents or close calls? If yes, please describe:

9. How often have taken the time to report minor accidents/incidents that didn't require immediate attention?
   Never Rarely Sometimes Often Always

10.
What do think is most effective way for us recognize and reward employees who demonstrate commitment health safety measures?

a) Public recognition
b)
c)

11.)
Have you ever felt uncomfortable reporting a workplace hazard or incident due to fear of repercussions? If yes, please explain:

12. How likely are willing participate in regular Health &amp; Safety training sessions?
   Not at all Somewhat Likely Very Unlikely Extremely

[LLM ANSWER]
Here's an initial draft for you:

**Onboarded Employee Questionnaire**

We value our employees' experiences at [Company Name] and want your feedback to improve future onboardings. Your input will help us refine the process, ensuring new hires feel welcome from day one.

Please answer these questions honestly; all responses are anonymous unless specified otherwise (marked with *).

**Section 1: Pre-Onboarding**

What was most exciting about joining [Company Name]?

* A specific job role or responsibilities
A company culture that aligns well to my values and interests

How did you prepare for your new position? 

I reviewed the employee handbook, familiarized myself online resources (e.g., training modules)
Spoke with colleagues/mentors beforehand; attended orientation sessions on day one*

What was most helpful in preparing me before starting work?

* A comprehensive job description
A detailed outline of expectations and goals

**Section 2: Onboarding Process**

How would you rate the overall effectiveness during your first week? (Scale from Very Effective to Not at All)

1. Introduction/Welcome by HR/Business Partner*
3 - Somewhat effective, but some areas for improvement were noticed.
5-6) Extremely or very helpful

What was most impressive about our onboarding process?

* Clear communication and transparency
A well-planned schedule with relevant training sessions*

Were there any aspects that could be improved? If yes:

Please specify: _______________________________________________________

**Section 3. Job Responsibilities & Training**

How would you rate the clarity of your job responsibilities during orientation/first week?
(Scale from Very Effective to Not at All)

1 - Extremely clear
2-4) Somewhat effective, but some areas for improvement were noticed.
5 or less: Needs significant clarification

What training sessions did we provide that helped most in getting started?

* Technical skills (e.g., software tools)
Soft Skills/Teamwork-oriented*

Were there any specific resources you found particularly helpful? If yes:

Please specify _______________________________________________________

**Section 4. Company Culture & Colleagues**

How would rate the overall company culture during your first week?
(Scale from Very Positive to Not at All)

1 - Extremely positive
2-3) Somewhat neutral, but some areas for improvement were noticed.
5 or less: Needs significant attention

What did you find most impressive about our team/colleagues?

* Friendly and approachable colleagues*
Clear communication among departments*

Were there any aspects that surprised/delighted/disappointed? If yes:

Please specify _______________________________________________________

**Section 4. Additional Feedback**

Do we have a chance to make [Company Name] an even better place for you in the future?
Yes, I'd be happy share more ideas!
No

Any additional comments or suggestions about your onboarding experience?

______________________________________________________________________________

Thank You!

Your input is invaluable!
